112// Error messages formerly used by viminfo code:
113// E136: viminfo: Too many errors, skipping rest of file
114// E137: Viminfo file is not writable: %s
115// E138: Can't write viminfo file %s!
116// E195: Cannot open ShaDa file for reading
117// E574: Unknown register type %d
118// E575: Illegal starting char
119// E576: Missing '>'
120// E577: Illegal register name
121// E886: Can't rename viminfo file to %s!
122// Now only six of them are used:
123// E137: ShaDa file is not writeable (for pre-open checks)
124// E138: All %s.tmp.X files exist, cannot write ShaDa file!
125// RCERR (E576) for critical read errors.
126// RNERR (E136) for various errors when renaming.
127// RERR (E575) for various errors inside read ShaDa file.
128// SERR (E886) for various system errors (always contains output of
129// strerror)
130// WERR (E574) for various ignorable write errors
131
132/// Common prefix for all errors inside ShaDa file
133///
134/// I.e. errors occurred while parsing, but not system errors occurred while
135/// reading.
136#define RERR"E575: " "E575: "
137
138/// Common prefix for critical read errors
139///
140/// I.e. errors that make shada_read_next_item return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa.
141#define RCERR"E576: " "E576: "
142
143/// Common prefix for all system errors
144#define SERR"E886: " "E886: "
145
146/// Common prefix for all rename errors
147#define RNERR"E136: " "E136: "
148
149/// Common prefix for all ignorable write errors
150#define WERR"E574: " "E574: "
151
152/// Flags for shada_read_file and children
153typedef enum {
154 kShaDaWantInfo = 1, ///< Load non-mark information
155 kShaDaWantMarks = 2, ///< Load local file marks and change list
156 kShaDaForceit = 4, ///< Overwrite info already read
157 kShaDaGetOldfiles = 8, ///< Load v:oldfiles.
158 kShaDaMissingError = 16, ///< Error out when os_open returns -ENOENT.
159} ShaDaReadFileFlags;
160
161/// Possible ShaDa entry types
162///
163/// @warning Enum values are part of the API and must not be altered.
164///
165/// All values that are not in enum are ignored.
166typedef enum {
167 kSDItemUnknown = -1, ///< Unknown item.
168 kSDItemMissing = 0, ///< Missing value. Should never appear in a file.
169 kSDItemHeader = 1, ///< Header. Present for debugging purposes.
170 kSDItemSearchPattern = 2, ///< Last search pattern (*not* history item).
171 ///< Comes from user searches (e.g. when typing
172 ///< "/pat") or :substitute command calls.
173 kSDItemSubString = 3, ///< Last substitute replacement string.
174 kSDItemHistoryEntry = 4, ///< History item.
175 kSDItemRegister = 5, ///< Register.
176 kSDItemVariable = 6, ///< Global variable.
177 kSDItemGlobalMark = 7, ///< Global mark definition.
178 kSDItemJump = 8, ///< Item from jump list.
179 kSDItemBufferList = 9, ///< Buffer list.
180 kSDItemLocalMark = 10, ///< Buffer-local mark.
181 kSDItemChange = 11, ///< Item from buffer change list.
182#define SHADA_LAST_ENTRY((uint64_t) kSDItemChange) ((uint64_t) kSDItemChange)
183} ShadaEntryType;
184
185/// Possible results when reading ShaDa file
186typedef enum {
187 kSDReadStatusSuccess, ///< Reading was successfull.
188 kSDReadStatusFinished, ///< Nothing more to read.
189 kSDReadStatusReadError, ///< Failed to read from file.
190 kSDReadStatusNotShaDa, ///< Input is most likely not a ShaDa file.
191 kSDReadStatusMalformed, ///< Error in the currently read item.
192} ShaDaReadResult;
193
194/// Possible results of shada_write function.
195typedef enum {
196 kSDWriteSuccessfull, ///< Writing was successfull.
197 kSDWriteReadNotShada, ///< Writing was successfull, but when reading it
198 ///< attempted to read file that did not look like
199 ///< a ShaDa file.
200 kSDWriteFailed, ///< Writing was not successfull (e.g. because there
201 ///< was no space left on device).
202 kSDWriteIgnError, ///< Writing resulted in a error which can be ignored
203 ///< (e.g. when trying to dump a function reference or
204 ///< self-referencing container in a variable).
205} ShaDaWriteResult;
206
207/// Flags for shada_read_next_item
208enum SRNIFlags {
209 kSDReadHeader = (1 << kSDItemHeader), ///< Determines whether header should
210 ///< be read (it is usually ignored).
211 kSDReadUndisableableData = (
212 (1 << kSDItemSearchPattern)
213 | (1 << kSDItemSubString)
214 | (1 << kSDItemJump)), ///< Data reading which cannot be disabled by
215 ///< &shada or other options except for disabling
216 ///< reading ShaDa as a whole.
217 kSDReadRegisters = (1 << kSDItemRegister), ///< Determines whether registers
218 ///< should be read (may only be
219 ///< disabled when writing, but
220 ///< not when reading).
221 kSDReadHistory = (1 << kSDItemHistoryEntry), ///< Determines whether history
222 ///< should be read (can only be
223 ///< disabled by &history).
224 kSDReadVariables = (1 << kSDItemVariable), ///< Determines whether variables
225 ///< should be read (disabled by
226 ///< removing ! from &shada).
227 kSDReadBufferList = (1 << kSDItemBufferList), ///< Determines whether buffer
228 ///< list should be read
229 ///< (disabled by removing
230 ///< % entry from &shada).
231 kSDReadUnknown = (1 << (SHADA_LAST_ENTRY((uint64_t) kSDItemChange) + 1)), ///< Determines whether
232 ///< unknown items should be
233 ///< read (usually disabled).
234 kSDReadGlobalMarks = (1 << kSDItemGlobalMark), ///< Determines whether global
235 ///< marks should be read. Can
236 ///< only be disabled by
237 ///< having f0 in &shada when
238 ///< writing.
239 kSDReadLocalMarks = (1 << kSDItemLocalMark), ///< Determines whether local
240 ///< marks should be read. Can
241 ///< only be disabled by
242 ///< disabling &shada or putting
243 ///< '0 there. Is also used for
244 ///< v:oldfiles.
245 kSDReadChanges = (1 << kSDItemChange), ///< Determines whether change list
246 ///< should be read. Can only be
247 ///< disabled by disabling &shada or
248 ///< putting '0 there.
249};
250// Note: SRNIFlags enum name was created only to make it possible to reference
251// it. This name is not actually used anywhere outside of the documentation.

522 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
523{
524 *hmll = (HMLList) {
525 .entries = xcalloc(size, sizeof(hmll->entries[0])),
526 .first = NULL((void*)0),
527 .last = NULL((void*)0),
528 .free_entry = NULL((void*)0),
529 .size = size,
530 .num_entries = 0,
531 .contained_entries = KHASH_EMPTY_TABLE(hmll_entries)((kh_hmll_entries_t) { .n_buckets = 0, .size = 0, .n_occupied
= 0, .upper_bound = 0, .flags = ((void*)0), .keys = ((void*)
0), .vals = ((void*)0), }),
532 };
533 hmll->last_free_entry = hmll->entries;
534}

662/// Wrapper for reading from file descriptors
663///
664/// @return -1 or number of bytes read.
665static ptrdiff_t read_file(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader, void *const dest,
666 const size_t size)
667 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
668{
669 size_t read_bytes = 0;
670 bool_Bool did_try_to_free = false0;
671 const int fd = (int)(intptr_t) sd_reader->cookie;
672 while (read_bytes != size) {
673 const ptrdiff_t cur_read_bytes = read(fd, ((char *) dest) + read_bytes,
674 size - read_bytes);
675 if (cur_read_bytes > 0) {
676 read_bytes += (size_t) cur_read_bytes;
677 sd_reader->fpos += (uintmax_t) cur_read_bytes;
678 assert(read_bytes <= size)((read_bytes <= size) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("read_bytes <= size"
, "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 678, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
679 }
680 if (cur_read_bytes < 0) {
681 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4 || errno(*__errno_location ()) == EAGAIN11) {
682 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
683 continue;
684 } else if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == ENOMEM12 && !did_try_to_free) {
685 try_to_free_memory();
686 did_try_to_free = true1;
687 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
688 continue;
689 } else {
690 sd_reader->error = strerror(errno(*__errno_location ()));
691 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
692 return -1;
693 }
694 }
695 if (cur_read_bytes == 0) {
696 sd_reader->eof = true1;
697 break;
698 }
699 }
700 return (ptrdiff_t) read_bytes;
701}
702
703/// Read one character
704static int read_char(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader)
705 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
706{
707 uint8_t ret;
708 ptrdiff_t read_bytes = sd_reader->read(sd_reader, &ret, 1);
709 if (read_bytes != 1) {
710 return EOF(-1);
711 }
712 return (int) ret;
713}
714
715/// Wrapper for writing to file descriptors
716///
717/// @return -1 or number of bytes written.
718static ptrdiff_t write_file(ShaDaWriteDef *const sd_writer,
719 const void *const dest,
720 const size_t size)
721 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
722{
723 size_t written_bytes = 0;
724 const int fd = (int)(intptr_t) sd_writer->cookie;
725 while (written_bytes != size) {
726 const ptrdiff_t cur_written_bytes = write(fd, (char *) dest + written_bytes,
727 size - written_bytes);
728 if (cur_written_bytes > 0) {
729 written_bytes += (size_t) cur_written_bytes;
730 }
731 if (cur_written_bytes < 0) {
732 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4 || errno(*__errno_location ()) == EAGAIN11) {
733 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
734 continue;
735 } else {
736 sd_writer->error = strerror(errno(*__errno_location ()));
737 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
738 return -1;
739 }
740 }
741 if (cur_written_bytes == 0) {
742 sd_writer->error = "Zero bytes written.";
743 return -1;
744 }
745 }
746 return (ptrdiff_t) written_bytes;
747}

751 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL

753 close_file((int)(intptr_t) sd_reader->cookie);
754}

756/// Wrapper for closing file descriptors opened for writing
757static void close_sd_writer(ShaDaWriteDef *const sd_writer)
758 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
759{
760 const int fd = (int)(intptr_t) sd_writer->cookie;
761 if (os_fsync(fd) < 0) {
762 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while synchronizing ShaDa file: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while synchronizing ShaDa file: %s"
)),
763 os_strerroruv_strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
764 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
765 }
766 close_file(fd);
767}

769/// Wrapper for read that reads to IObuff and ignores bytes read
770///
771/// Used for skipping.
772///
773/// @param[in,out] sd_reader File read.
774/// @param[in] offset Amount of bytes to skip.
775///
776/// @return FAIL in case of failure, OK in case of success. May set
777/// sd_reader->eof or sd_reader->error.
778static int sd_reader_skip_read(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader,
779 const size_t offset)
780 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
781{
782 size_t read_bytes = 0;
783 do {
784 ptrdiff_t new_read_bytes = sd_reader->read(
785 sd_reader, IObuff, (size_t) (offset - read_bytes > IOSIZE(1024+1)
786 ? IOSIZE(1024+1)
787 : offset - read_bytes));
788 if (new_read_bytes == -1) {
789 return FAIL0;
790 }
791 read_bytes += (size_t) new_read_bytes;
792 } while (read_bytes < offset && !sd_reader->eof);
793
794 return (read_bytes == offset ? OK1 : FAIL0);
795}

797/// Wrapper for read that can be used when lseek cannot be used

812 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while skipping in ShaDa file: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while skipping in ShaDa file: %s"
)),
813 sd_reader->error);
814 return kSDReadStatusReadError;
815 } else if (sd_reader->eof) {
816 emsgf(_(RCERR "Error while reading ShaDa file: "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier"))
817 "last entry specified that it occupies %" PRIu64 " bytes, "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier"))
818 "but file ended earlier")gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier")),
819 (uint64_t) offset);
820 return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
821 }
822 assert(false)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 822, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));

827/// Wrapper for opening file descriptors
828///
829/// All arguments are passed to os_open().
830///
831/// @return file descriptor or libuv error on failure.
832static int open_file(const char *const fname, const int flags, const int mode)
833 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
834{
835 bool_Bool did_try_to_free = false0;
836 int fd;
837open_file_start:
838 fd = os_open(fname, flags, mode);
839
840 if (fd < 0) {
841 if (fd == UV_ENOENT) {
842 return fd;
843 }
844 if (fd == UV_ENOMEM && !did_try_to_free) {
845 try_to_free_memory();
846 did_try_to_free = true1;
847 goto open_file_start;
848 }
849 if (fd != UV_EEXIST) {
850 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while opening ShaDa file %s: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while opening ShaDa file %s: %s"
)),
851 fname, os_strerroruv_strerror(fd));
852 }
853 return fd;
854 }
855 return fd;
856}

858/// Open ShaDa file for reading
859///
860/// @param[in] fname File name to open.
861/// @param[out] sd_reader Location where reader structure will be saved.
862///
863/// @return libuv error in case of error, 0 otherwise.
864static int open_shada_file_for_reading(const char *const fname,
865 ShaDaReadDef *sd_reader)
866 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
867{
868 const intptr_t fd = (intptr_t) open_file(fname, O_RDONLY00, 0);
869
870 if (fd < 0) {
871 return (int) fd;
872 }
873
874 *sd_reader = (ShaDaReadDef) {
875 .read = &read_file,
876 .close = &close_sd_reader,
877 .skip = &sd_reader_skip_read,
878 .error = NULL((void*)0),
879 .eof = false0,
880 .fpos = 0,
881 .cookie = (void *) fd,
882 };
883
884 convert_setup(&sd_reader->sd_conv, "utf-8", p_enc)(convert_setup(&sd_reader->sd_conv, (char_u *)"utf-8",
(char_u *)p_enc));
885
886 return 0;
887}

889/// Wrapper for closing file descriptors
890static void close_file(int fd)
891{
892close_file_start:
893 if (close(fd) == -1) {
894 if (errno(*__errno_location ()) == EINTR4) {
895 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
896 goto close_file_start;
897 } else {
898 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while closing ShaDa file: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while closing ShaDa file: %s"
)),
899 strerror(errno(*__errno_location ())));
900 errno(*__errno_location ()) = 0;
901 }
902 }
903}

951/// Read ShaDa file
952///
953/// @param[in] file File to read or NULL to use default name.
954/// @param[in] flags Flags, see ShaDaReadFileFlags enum.
955///
956/// @return FAIL if reading failed for some reason and OK otherwise.
957static int shada_read_file(const char *const file, const int flags)
958 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
959{
960 if (shada_disabled()) {
961 return FAIL0;
962 }
963
964 char *const fname = shada_filename(file);
965
966 ShaDaReadDef sd_reader;
967 const int of_ret = open_shada_file_for_reading(fname, &sd_reader);
968
969 if (p_verbose > 0) {
970 verbose_enter();
971 smsg(_("Reading ShaDa file \"%s\"%s%s%s")gettext((char *)("Reading ShaDa file \"%s\"%s%s%s")),
972 fname,
973 (flags & kShaDaWantInfo) ? _(" info")gettext((char *)(" info")) : "",
974 (flags & kShaDaWantMarks) ? _(" marks")gettext((char *)(" marks")) : "",
975 (flags & kShaDaGetOldfiles) ? _(" oldfiles")gettext((char *)(" oldfiles")) : "",
976 of_ret != 0 ? _(" FAILED")gettext((char *)(" FAILED")) : "");
977 verbose_leave();
978 }
979
980 if (of_ret != 0) {
981 if (of_ret == UV_ENOENT && (flags & kShaDaMissingError)) {
982 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while opening ShaDa file %s for reading: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while opening ShaDa file %s for reading: %s"
)),
983 fname, os_strerroruv_strerror(of_ret));
984 }
985 xfree(fname);
986 return FAIL0;
987 }
988 xfree(fname);
989
990 shada_read(&sd_reader, flags);
991 sd_reader.close(&sd_reader);
992
993 return OK1;
994}

996/// Wrapper for hist_iter() function which produces ShadaEntry values

1005static const void *shada_hist_iter(const void *const iter,

1010{

1018 .timestamp = hist_he.timestamp,

1020 .history_item = {
1021 .histtype = history_type,
1022 .string = (char *) hist_he.hisstr,
1023 .sep = (char) (history_type == HIST_SEARCH
1024 ? (char) hist_he.hisstr[STRLEN(hist_he.hisstr)strlen((char *)(hist_he.hisstr)) + 1]
1025 : 0),
1026 .additional_elements = hist_he.additional_elements,
1027 }
1028 }
1029 };
1030 }
1031 return ret;
1032}

1034/// Insert history entry
1035///
1036/// Inserts history entry at the end of the ring buffer (may insert earlier
1037/// according to the timestamp). If entry was already in the ring buffer
1038/// existing entry will be removed unless it has greater timestamp.
1039///
1040/// Before the new entry entries from the current Neovim history will be
1041/// inserted unless `do_iter` argument is false.
1042///
1043/// @param[in,out] hms_p Ring buffer and associated structures.
1044/// @param[in] entry Inserted entry.
1045/// @param[in] do_iter Determines whether Neovim own history should
1046/// be used. Must be true only if inserting
1047/// entry from current Neovim history.
1048/// @param[in] can_free_entry True if entry can be freed.
1049static void hms_insert(HistoryMergerState *const hms_p, const ShadaEntry entry,
1050 const bool_Bool do_iter, const bool_Bool can_free_entry)
1051 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
1052{
1053 if (do_iter) {

1055 && hms_p->last_hist_entry.timestamp < entry.timestamp) {

1057 if (hms_p->iter == NULL((void*)0)) {
1058 hms_p->last_hist_entry.type = kSDItemMissing;
1059 break;
1060 }
1061 hms_p->iter = shada_hist_iter(hms_p->iter, hms_p->history_type,
1062 hms_p->reading, &hms_p->last_hist_entry);

.data.history_item.string)

.data.history_item.string);

1069 HMLListEntry *const existing_entry = kh_val(&hmll->contained_entries, k)((&hmll->contained_entries)->vals[k]);
1070 if (entry.timestamp > existing_entry->data.timestamp) {
1071 hmll_remove(hmll, existing_entry);
1072 } else if (!do_iter && entry.timestamp == existing_entry->data.timestamp) {
1073 // Prefer entry from the current Neovim instance.
1074 if (existing_entry->can_free_entry) {
1075 shada_free_shada_entry(&existing_entry->data);
1076 }
1077 existing_entry->data = entry;
1078 existing_entry->can_free_entry = can_free_entry;
1079 // Previous key was freed above, as part of freeing the ShaDa entry.
1080 kh_key(&hmll->contained_entries, k)((&hmll->contained_entries)->keys[k]) = entry.data.history_item.string;
1081 return;
1082 } else {
1083 return;
1084 }
1085 }
1086 HMLListEntry *insert_after;
1087 HMLL_ITER_BACK(hmll, insert_after, {for (insert_after = (hmll)->last; insert_after != ((void*)

1095/// Initialize the history merger
1096///
1097/// @param[out] hms_p Structure to be initialized.
1098/// @param[in] history_type History type (one of HIST_\* values).
1099/// @param[in] num_elements Number of elements in the result.
1100/// @param[in] do_merge Prepare structure for merging elements.
1101/// @param[in] reading If true, then merger is reading history for use
1102/// in Neovim.
1103static inline void hms_init(HistoryMergerState *const hms_p,
1104 const uint8_t history_type,
1105 const size_t num_elements,
1106 const bool_Bool do_merge,
1107 const bool_Bool reading)
1108 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
1109{
1110 hmll_init(&hms_p->hmll, num_elements);
1111 hms_p->do_merge = do_merge;
1112 hms_p->reading = reading;
1113 hms_p->iter = shada_hist_iter(NULL((void*)0), history_type, hms_p->reading,
1114 &hms_p->last_hist_entry);
1115 hms_p->history_type = history_type;
1116}

1118/// Merge in all remaining Neovim own history entries
1119///
1120/// @param[in,out] hms_p Merger structure into which history should be
1121/// inserted.
1122static inline void hms_insert_whole_neovim_history(
1123 HistoryMergerState *const hms_p)
1124 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
1125{
1126 while (hms_p->last_hist_entry.type != kSDItemMissing) {
1127 hms_insert(hms_p, hms_p->last_hist_entry, false0, hms_p->reading);
1128 if (hms_p->iter == NULL((void*)0)) {
1129 break;
1130 }
1131 hms_p->iter = shada_hist_iter(hms_p->iter, hms_p->history_type,
1132 hms_p->reading, &hms_p->last_hist_entry);
1133 }
1134}

== 100) { i = -1; } else if (jl_len > 0) { memmove(&buf
->b_changelist[1], &buf->b_changelist[0], sizeof(buf
->b_changelist[0]) * (size_t) jl_len); } } if (i != -1) { buf
->b_changelist[i] = SDE_TO_FMARK(cur_entry); if (jl_len <
100) { buf->b_changelistlen++; } DUMMY_IDX_ADJ(i); } else
{ shada_free_shada_entry(&cur_entry); AFTERFREE(cur_entry
); } } while (0);
1556#undef SDE_TO_FMARK
1557#undef AFTERFREE
1558#undef DUMMY_IDX_ADJ
1559 }
1560 // Do not free shada entry: except for fname, its allocated memory (i.e.
1561 // additional_data attribute contents if non-NULL) was saved above.
1562 xfree(cur_entry.data.filemark.fname);
1563 break;
1564 }
1565 }
1566 }
1567shada_read_main_cycle_end:
1568 // Warning: shada_hist_iter returns ShadaEntry elements which use strings from
1569 // original history list. This means that once such entry is removed
1570 // from the history Neovim array will no longer be valid. To reduce
1571 // amount of memory allocations ShaDa file reader allocates enough
1572 // memory for the history string itself and separator character which
1573 // may be assigned right away.
1574 if (srni_flags & kSDReadHistory) {
1575 for (uint8_t i = 0; i < HIST_COUNT(HIST_DEBUG + 1); i++) {
1576 hms_insert_whole_neovim_history(&hms[i]);
1577 clr_history(i);
1578 int *new_hisidx;
1579 int *new_hisnum;
1580 histentry_T *hist = hist_get_array(i, &new_hisidx, &new_hisnum);
1581 if (hist != NULL((void*)0)) {
1582 hms_to_he_array(&hms[i], hist, new_hisidx, new_hisnum);
1583 }
1584 hms_dealloc(&hms[i]);
1585 }
1586 }
1587 if (cl_bufs.n_occupied) {
1588 FOR_ALL_TAB_WINDOWS(tp, wp)for (tabpage_T *tp = first_tabpage; tp != ((void*)0); tp = tp
->tp_next) for (win_T *wp = ((tp) == curtab) ? firstwin : (
tp)->tp_firstwin; wp != ((void*)0); wp = wp->w_next) {
1589 (void) tp;
1590 if (in_bufset(&cl_bufs, wp->w_buffer)) {
1591 wp->w_changelistidx = wp->w_buffer->b_changelistlen;
1592 }
1593 }
1594 }
1595 kh_dealloc(bufset, &cl_bufs)kh_dealloc_bufset(&cl_bufs);
1596 const char *key;
1597 kh_foreach_key(&fname_bufs, key, {{ khint_t __i; for (__i = (khint_t)(0); __i != ((&fname_bufs
)->n_buckets); __i++) { if (!(!(((&fname_bufs)->flags
[(__i)>>4]>>(((__i)&0xfU)<<1))&3)))
{ continue; } (key) = ((&fname_bufs)->keys[__i]); { xfree
((void *) key); }; } }
1598 xfree((void *) key);{ khint_t __i; for (__i = (khint_t)(0); __i != ((&fname_bufs

1604/// Default shada file location: cached path
1605static char *default_shada_file = NULL((void*)0);
1606
1607/// Get the default ShaDa file
1608static const char *shada_get_default_file(void)
1609 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
1610{
1611 if (default_shada_file == NULL((void*)0)) {
1612 char *shada_dir = stdpaths_user_data_subpath("shada", 0);
1613 default_shada_file = concat_fnames_realloc(shada_dir, "main.shada", true1);
1614 }
1615 return default_shada_file;
1616}
1617
1618/// Get the ShaDa file name to use
1619///
1620/// If "file" is given and not empty, use it (has already been expanded by
1621/// cmdline functions). Otherwise use "-i file_name", value from 'shada' or the
1622/// default, and expand environment variables.
1623///
1624/// @param[in] file Forced file name or NULL.
1625///
1626/// @return An allocated string containing shada file name.
1627static char *shada_filename(const char *file)
1628 FUNC_ATTR_MALLOC FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_RET FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
1629{
1630 if (file == NULL((void*)0) || *file == NUL'\000') {
1631 if (used_shada_file != NULL((void*)0)) {
1632 file = used_shada_file;
1633 } else {
1634 if ((file = find_shada_parameter('n')((const char *) find_shada_parameter('n'))) == NULL((void*)0) || *file == NUL'\000') {
1635 file = shada_get_default_file();
1636 }
1637 // XXX It used to be one level lower, so that whatever is in
1638 // `used_shada_file` was expanded. I intentionally moved it here
1639 // because various expansions must have already be done by the shell.
1640 // If shell is not performing them then they should be done in main.c
1641 // where arguments are parsed, *not here*.
1642 expand_env((char_u *)file, &(NameBuff[0]), MAXPATHL4096);
1643 file = (const char *) &(NameBuff[0]);
1644 }
1645 }
1646 return xstrdup(file);
1647}

1659 } while (0)

); msgpack_pack_bin_body(spacker, s_.data, s_.size); } while (
0) \
1661 do { \

1667/// Write single ShaDa entry

1982/// Write single ShaDa entry, converting it if needed
1983///
1984/// @warning Frees entry after packing.
1985///
1986/// @param[in] packer Packer used to write entry.
1987/// @param[in] sd_conv Conversion definitions.
1988/// @param[in] entry Entry written. If entry.can_free_entry is false then
1989/// it assumes that entry was not converted, otherwise it
1990/// is assumed that entry was already converted.
1991/// @param[in] max_kbyte Maximum size of an item in KiB. Zero means no
1992/// restrictions.
1993static ShaDaWriteResult shada_pack_encoded_entry(msgpack_packer *const packer,
1994 const vimconv_T *const sd_conv,
1995 PossiblyFreedShadaEntry entry,
1996 const size_t max_kbyte)
1997 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL
1998{
1999 ShaDaWriteResult ret = kSDWriteSuccessfull;
2000 if (entry.can_free_entry) {
2001 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2002 shada_free_shada_entry(&entry.data);
2003 return ret;
2004 }
2005#define RUN_WITH_CONVERTED_STRING(cstr, code) \
2006 do { \
2007 bool_Bool did_convert = false0; \
2008 if (sd_conv->vc_type != CONV_NONE0 && has_non_ascii((cstr))(has_non_ascii((char_u *)(cstr)))) { \
2009 char *const converted_string = string_convert(sd_conv, (cstr), NULL)((char *)string_convert((vimconv_T *)sd_conv, (char_u *)(cstr
), ((void*)0))); \
2010 if (converted_string != NULL((void*)0)) { \
2011 (cstr) = converted_string; \
2012 did_convert = true1; \
2013 } \
2014 } \
2015 code \
2016 if (did_convert) { \
2017 xfree((cstr)); \
2018 } \
2019 } while (0)
2020 switch (entry.data.type) {
2021 case kSDItemUnknown:
2022 case kSDItemMissing: {
2023 assert(false)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 2023, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2024 }
2025 case kSDItemSearchPattern: {
2026 RUN_WITH_CONVERTED_STRING(entry.data.data.search_pattern.pat, {
2027 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2028 });
2029 break;
2030 }
2031 case kSDItemHistoryEntry: {
2032 RUN_WITH_CONVERTED_STRING(entry.data.data.history_item.string, {
2033 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2034 });
2035 break;
2036 }
2037 case kSDItemSubString: {
2038 RUN_WITH_CONVERTED_STRING(entry.data.data.sub_string.sub, {
2039 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2040 });
2041 break;
2042 }
2043 case kSDItemVariable: {
2044 if (sd_conv->vc_type != CONV_NONE0) {
2045 typval_T tgttv;
2046 var_item_copy(sd_conv, &entry.data.data.global_var.value, &tgttv,
2047 true1, 0);
2048 clear_tv(&entry.data.data.global_var.value);
2049 entry.data.data.global_var.value = tgttv;
2050 }
2051 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2052 break;
2053 }
2054 case kSDItemRegister: {
2055 bool_Bool did_convert = false0;
2056 if (sd_conv->vc_type != CONV_NONE0) {
2057 size_t first_non_ascii = 0;
2058 for (size_t i = 0; i < entry.data.data.reg.contents_size; i++) {
2059 if (has_non_ascii(entry.data.data.reg.contents[i])(has_non_ascii((char_u *)entry.data.data.reg.contents[i]))) {
2060 first_non_ascii = i;
2061 did_convert = true1;
2062 break;
2063 }
2064 }
2065 if (did_convert) {
2066 entry.data.data.reg.contents =
2067 xmemdup(entry.data.data.reg.contents,
2068 (entry.data.data.reg.contents_size
2069 * sizeof(entry.data.data.reg.contents)));
2070 for (size_t i = 0; i < entry.data.data.reg.contents_size; i++) {
2071 if (i >= first_non_ascii) {
2072 entry.data.data.reg.contents[i] = get_converted_string(
2073 sd_conv,
2074 entry.data.data.reg.contents[i],
2075 strlen(entry.data.data.reg.contents[i]));
2076 } else {
2077 entry.data.data.reg.contents[i] =
2078 xstrdup(entry.data.data.reg.contents[i]);
2079 }
2080 }
2081 }
2082 }
2083 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2084 if (did_convert) {
2085 for (size_t i = 0; i < entry.data.data.reg.contents_size; i++) {
2086 xfree(entry.data.data.reg.contents[i]);
2087 }
2088 xfree(entry.data.data.reg.contents);
2089 }
2090 break;
2091 }
2092 case kSDItemHeader:
2093 case kSDItemGlobalMark:
2094 case kSDItemJump:
2095 case kSDItemBufferList:
2096 case kSDItemLocalMark:
2097 case kSDItemChange: {
2098 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry.data, max_kbyte);
2099 break;
2100 }
2101 }
2102#undef RUN_WITH_CONVERTED_STRING
2103 return ret;
2104}

2106/// Compare two FileMarks structure to order them by greatest_timestamp
2107///
2108/// Order is reversed: structure with greatest greatest_timestamp comes first.
2109/// Function signature is compatible with qsort.
2110static int compare_file_marks(const void *a, const void *b)
2111 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT FUNC_ATTR_PURE
2112{
2113 const FileMarks *const *const a_fms = a;
2114 const FileMarks *const *const b_fms = b;
2115 return ((*a_fms)->greatest_timestamp == (*b_fms)->greatest_timestamp
2116 ? 0
2117 : ((*a_fms)->greatest_timestamp > (*b_fms)->greatest_timestamp
2118 ? -1
2119 : 1));
2120}

2122/// Parse msgpack object that has given length
2123///
2124/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition.
2125/// @param[in] length Object length.
2126/// @param[out] ret_unpacked Location where read result should be saved. If
2127/// NULL then unpacked data will be freed. Must be
2128/// NULL if `ret_buf` is NULL.
2129/// @param[out] ret_buf Buffer containing parsed string.
2130///
2131/// @return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa, kSDReadStatusReadError or
2132/// kSDReadStatusSuccess.
2133static inline ShaDaReadResult shada_parse_msgpack(
2134 ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader, const size_t length,
2135 msgpack_unpacked *ret_unpacked, char **const ret_buf)
2136 FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ARG(1)
2137{
2138 const uintmax_t initial_fpos = sd_reader->fpos;
2139 char *const buf = xmalloc(length);
2140
2141 const ShaDaReadResult fl_ret = fread_len(sd_reader, buf, length);
2142 if (fl_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
2143 xfree(buf);
2144 return fl_ret;
2145 }
2146 bool_Bool did_try_to_free = false0;
2147shada_parse_msgpack_read_next: {}
2148 size_t off = 0;
2149 msgpack_unpacked unpacked;
2150 msgpack_unpacked_init(&unpacked);
2151 const msgpack_unpack_return result =
2152 msgpack_unpack_next(&unpacked, buf, length, &off);
2153 ShaDaReadResult ret = kSDReadStatusSuccess;
2154 switch (result) {
2155 case MSGPACK_UNPACK_SUCCESS: {
2156 if (off < length) {
2157 goto shada_parse_msgpack_extra_bytes;
2158 }
2159 break;
2160 }
2161 case MSGPACK_UNPACK_PARSE_ERROR: {
2162 emsgf(_(RCERR "Failed to parse ShaDa file due to a msgpack parser error "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file due to a msgpack parser error "
"at position %" "l" "u"))
2163 "at position %" PRIu64)gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file due to a msgpack parser error "
"at position %" "l" "u")),
2164 (uint64_t) initial_fpos);
2165 ret = kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
2166 break;
2167 }
2168 case MSGPACK_UNPACK_NOMEM_ERROR: {
2169 if (!did_try_to_free) {
2170 did_try_to_free = true1;
2171 try_to_free_memory();
2172 goto shada_parse_msgpack_read_next;
2173 }
2174 EMSG(_(e_outofmem))emsg((char_u *)(gettext((char *)(e_outofmem))));
2175 ret = kSDReadStatusReadError;
2176 break;
2177 }
2178 case MSGPACK_UNPACK_CONTINUE: {
2179 emsgf(_(RCERR "Failed to parse ShaDa file: incomplete msgpack string "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file: incomplete msgpack string "
"at position %" "l" "u"))
2180 "at position %" PRIu64)gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file: incomplete msgpack string "
"at position %" "l" "u")),
2181 (uint64_t) initial_fpos);
2182 ret = kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
2183 break;
2184 }
2185 case MSGPACK_UNPACK_EXTRA_BYTES: {
2186shada_parse_msgpack_extra_bytes:
2187 emsgf(_(RCERR "Failed to parse ShaDa file: extra bytes in msgpack string "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file: extra bytes in msgpack string "
"at position %" "l" "u"))
2188 "at position %" PRIu64)gettext((char *)("E576: " "Failed to parse ShaDa file: extra bytes in msgpack string "
"at position %" "l" "u")),
2189 (uint64_t) initial_fpos);
2190 ret = kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
2191 break;
2192 }
2193 }
2194 if (ret_buf != NULL((void*)0) && ret == kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
2195 if (ret_unpacked == NULL((void*)0)) {
2196 msgpack_unpacked_destroy(&unpacked);
2197 } else {
2198 *ret_unpacked = unpacked;
2199 }
2200 *ret_buf = buf;
2201 } else {
2202 assert(ret_buf == NULL || ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess)((ret_buf == ((void*)0) || ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) ? (void
) (0) : __assert_fail ("ret_buf == ((void*)0) || ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess"
, "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 2202, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2203 msgpack_unpacked_destroy(&unpacked);
2204 xfree(buf);
2205 }
2206 return ret;
2207}
2208
2209/// Read and merge in ShaDa file, used when writing
2210///
2211/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition.
2212/// @param[in] srni_flags Flags determining what to read.
2213/// @param[in] max_kbyte Maximum size of one element.
2214/// @param[in,out] ret_wms Location where results are saved.
2215/// @param[out] packer MessagePack packer for entries which are not
2216/// merged.
2217static inline ShaDaWriteResult shada_read_when_writing(
2218 ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader, const unsigned srni_flags,
2219 const size_t max_kbyte, WriteMergerState *const wms,
2220 msgpack_packer *const packer)
2221 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
2222{
2223 ShaDaWriteResult ret = kSDWriteSuccessfull;
2224 ShadaEntry entry;
2225 ShaDaReadResult srni_ret;
2226 while ((srni_ret = shada_read_next_item(sd_reader, &entry, srni_flags,
2227 max_kbyte))
2228 != kSDReadStatusFinished) {
2229 switch (srni_ret) {
2230 case kSDReadStatusSuccess: {
2231 break;
2232 }
2233 case kSDReadStatusFinished: {
2234 // Should be handled by the while condition.
2235 assert(false)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 2235, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2236 }
2237 case kSDReadStatusNotShaDa: {
2238 ret = kSDWriteReadNotShada;
2239 // fallthrough
2240 }
2241 case kSDReadStatusReadError: {
2242 return ret;
2243 }
2244 case kSDReadStatusMalformed: {
2245 continue;
2246 }
2247 }
2248#define COMPARE_WITH_ENTRY(wms_entry_, entry) \
2249 do { \
2250 PossiblyFreedShadaEntry *const wms_entry = (wms_entry_); \
2251 if (wms_entry->data.type != kSDItemMissing) { \
2252 if (wms_entry->data.timestamp >= (entry).timestamp) { \
2253 shada_free_shada_entry(&(entry)); \
2254 break; \
2255 } \
2256 if (wms_entry->can_free_entry) { \
2257 shada_free_shada_entry(&wms_entry->data); \
2258 } \
2259 } \
2260 wms_entry->can_free_entry = true1; \
2261 wms_entry->data = (entry); \
2262 } while (0)
2263 switch (entry.type) {
2264 case kSDItemMissing: {
2265 break;
2266 }
2267 case kSDItemHeader:
2268 case kSDItemBufferList: {
2269 assert(false)((0) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("0", "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 2269, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
2270 }
2271 case kSDItemUnknown: {
2272 ret = shada_pack_entry(packer, entry, 0);
2273 shada_free_shada_entry(&entry);
2274 break;
2275 }
2276 case kSDItemSearchPattern: {
2277 COMPARE_WITH_ENTRY((entry.data.search_pattern.is_substitute_pattern
2278 ? &wms->sub_search_pattern
2279 : &wms->search_pattern), entry);
2280 break;
2281 }
2282 case kSDItemSubString: {
2283 COMPARE_WITH_ENTRY(&wms->replacement, entry);
2284 break;
2285 }
2286 case kSDItemHistoryEntry: {
2287 if (entry.data.history_item.histtype >= HIST_COUNT(HIST_DEBUG + 1)) {

2404
2405/// Write ShaDa file
2406///
2407/// @param[in] sd_writer Structure containing file writer definition.
2408/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition. If it is
2409/// not NULL then contents of this file will be merged
2410/// with current Neovim runtime.
2411static ShaDaWriteResult shada_write(ShaDaWriteDef *const sd_writer,
2412 ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader)
2413 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ARG(1)
2414{
2415 ShaDaWriteResult ret = kSDWriteSuccessfull;
2416 int max_kbyte_i = get_shada_parameter('s');
2417 if (max_kbyte_i < 0) {
2418 max_kbyte_i = 10;
2419 }
2420 if (max_kbyte_i == 0) {
2421 return ret;
2422 }
2423
2424 WriteMergerState *const wms = xcalloc(1, sizeof(*wms));
2425 bool_Bool dump_one_history[HIST_COUNT(HIST_DEBUG + 1)];
2426 const bool_Bool dump_global_vars = (find_shada_parameter('!')((const char *) find_shada_parameter('!')) != NULL((void*)0));
2427 int max_reg_lines = get_shada_parameter('<');
2428 if (max_reg_lines < 0) {
2429 max_reg_lines = get_shada_parameter('"');
2430 }
2431 const bool_Bool limit_reg_lines = max_reg_lines >= 0;
2432 const bool_Bool dump_registers = (max_reg_lines != 0);
2433 khash_t(bufset)kh_bufset_t removable_bufs = KHASH_EMPTY_TABLE(bufset)((kh_bufset_t) { .n_buckets = 0, .size = 0, .n_occupied = 0, .
upper_bound = 0, .flags = ((void*)0), .keys = ((void*)0), .vals
= ((void*)0), });
2434 const size_t max_kbyte = (size_t) max_kbyte_i;
2435 const size_t num_marked_files = (size_t) get_shada_parameter('\'');
2436 const bool_Bool dump_global_marks = get_shada_parameter('f') != 0;
2437 bool_Bool dump_history = false0;
2438
2439 // Initialize history merger
2440 for (uint8_t i = 0; i < HIST_COUNT(HIST_DEBUG + 1); i++) {
2441 long num_saved = get_shada_parameter(hist_type2char(i));
2442 if (num_saved == -1) {
2443 num_saved = p_hi;
2444 }
2445 if (num_saved > 0) {
2446 dump_history = true1;
2447 dump_one_history[i] = true1;
2448 hms_init(&wms->hms[i], i, (size_t) num_saved, sd_reader != NULL((void*)0), false0);
2449 } else {
2450 dump_one_history[i] = false0;
2451 }
2452 }
2453
2454 const unsigned srni_flags = (unsigned) (
2455 kSDReadUndisableableData
2456 | kSDReadUnknown
2457 | (dump_history ? kSDReadHistory : 0)
2458 | (dump_registers ? kSDReadRegisters : 0)
2459 | (dump_global_vars ? kSDReadVariables : 0)
2460 | (dump_global_marks ? kSDReadGlobalMarks : 0)
2461 | (num_marked_files ? kSDReadLocalMarks | kSDReadChanges : 0));
2462
2463 msgpack_packer *const packer = msgpack_packer_new(sd_writer,
2464 &msgpack_sd_writer_write);
2465
2466 // Set b_last_cursor for all the buffers that have a window.
2467 //
2468 // It is needed to correctly save '"' mark on exit. Has a side effect of
2469 // setting '"' mark in all windows on :wshada to the current cursor
2470 // position (basically what :wviminfo used to do).
2471 FOR_ALL_TAB_WINDOWS(tp, wp)for (tabpage_T *tp = first_tabpage; tp != ((void*)0); tp = tp
->tp_next) for (win_T *wp = ((tp) == curtab) ? firstwin : (
tp)->tp_firstwin; wp != ((void*)0); wp = wp->w_next) {
2472 set_last_cursor(wp);

hmll))->first; cur_entry != ((void*)0); cur_entry = cur_entry
->next) { { if (shada_pack_encoded_entry( packer, &sd_writer
->sd_conv, (PossiblyFreedShadaEntry) { .data = cur_entry->
data, .can_free_entry = cur_entry->can_free_entry, }, max_kbyte
) == kSDWriteFailed) { ret = kSDWriteFailed; break; } } }

2956/// Write ShaDa file to a given location
2957///
2958/// @param[in] fname File to write to. If it is NULL or empty then default
2959/// location is used.
2960/// @param[in] nomerge If true then old file is ignored.
2961///
2962/// @return OK if writing was successfull, FAIL otherwise.
2963int shada_write_file(const char *const file, bool_Bool nomerge)
2964{
2965 if (shada_disabled()) {
2966 return FAIL0;
2967 }
2968
2969 char *const fname = shada_filename(file);
2970 char *tempname = NULL((void*)0);
2971 ShaDaWriteDef sd_writer = (ShaDaWriteDef) {
2972 .write = &write_file,
2973 .close = &close_sd_writer,
2974 .error = NULL((void*)0),
2975 };
2976 ShaDaReadDef sd_reader;
2977
2978 intptr_t fd;
2979
2980 if (!nomerge) {
2981 if (open_shada_file_for_reading(fname, &sd_reader) != 0) {
2982 nomerge = true1;
2983 goto shada_write_file_nomerge;
2984 }
2985 tempname = modname(fname, ".tmp.a", false0);
2986 if (tempname == NULL((void*)0)) {
2987 nomerge = true1;
2988 goto shada_write_file_nomerge;
2989 }
2990
2991 // Save permissions from the original file, with modifications:
2992 int perm = (int) os_getperm(fname)(os_getperm((char_u *) fname));
2993 perm = (perm >= 0) ? ((perm & 0777) | 0600) : 0600;
2994 // ^3 ^1 ^2 ^2,3
2995 // 1: Strip SUID bit if any.
2996 // 2: Make sure that user can always read and write the result.
2997 // 3: If somebody happened to delete the file after it was opened for
2998 // reading use u=rw permissions.
2999shada_write_file_open:
3000 fd = (intptr_t) open_file(tempname, O_CREAT0100|O_WRONLY01|O_NOFOLLOW0400000|O_EXCL0200,
3001 perm);
3002 if (fd < 0) {
3003 if (fd == UV_EEXIST
3004#ifdef ELOOP40
3005 || fd == UV_ELOOP
3006#endif
3007 ) {
3008 // File already exists, try another name
3009 char *const wp = tempname + strlen(tempname) - 1;
3010 if (*wp == 'z') {
3011 // Tried names from .tmp.a to .tmp.z, all failed. Something must be
3012 // wrong then.
3013 EMSG2(_("E138: All %s.tmp.X files exist, cannot write ShaDa file!"),emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E138: All %s.tmp.X files exist, cannot write ShaDa file!"
))), (fname))

))), (fname));
3015 xfree(fname);
3016 xfree(tempname);
3017 return FAIL0;
3018 } else {
3019 (*wp)++;
3020 goto shada_write_file_open;
3021 }
3022 }
3023 }
3024 }
3025 if (nomerge) {
3026shada_write_file_nomerge: {}
3027 char *const tail = path_tail_with_sep(fname)((char *) path_tail_with_sep((char_u *)fname));
3028 if (tail != fname) {
3029 const char tail_save = *tail;
3030 *tail = NUL'\000';
3031 if (!os_isdir(fname)(os_isdir((char_u *) fname))) {
3032 int ret;
3033 char *failed_dir;
3034 if ((ret = os_mkdir_recurse(fname, 0700, &failed_dir)) != 0) {

"for writing ShaDa file: %s"))), (failed_dir), (uv_strerror(
ret)))
3036 "for writing ShaDa file: %s"),emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E886: " "Failed to create directory %s "
"for writing ShaDa file: %s"))), (failed_dir), (uv_strerror(
ret)))
3037 failed_dir, os_strerror(ret))emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E886: " "Failed to create directory %s "
"for writing ShaDa file: %s"))), (failed_dir), (uv_strerror(
ret)));
3038 xfree(fname);
3039 xfree(failed_dir);
3040 return FAIL0;
3041 }
3042 }
3043 *tail = tail_save;
3044 }
3045 fd = (intptr_t) open_file(fname, O_CREAT0100|O_WRONLY01|O_TRUNC01000,
3046 0600);
3047 }
3048
3049 if (p_verbose > 0) {
3050 verbose_enter();
3051 smsg(_("Writing ShaDa file \"%s\"")gettext((char *)("Writing ShaDa file \"%s\"")), fname);
3052 verbose_leave();
3053 }
3054
3055 if (fd < 0) {
3056 xfree(fname);
3057 xfree(tempname);
3058 return FAIL0;
3059 }
3060
3061 sd_writer.cookie = (void *) fd;
3062
3063 convert_setup(&sd_writer.sd_conv, p_enc, "utf-8")(convert_setup(&sd_writer.sd_conv, (char_u *)p_enc, (char_u
*)"utf-8"));
3064
3065 const ShaDaWriteResult sw_ret = shada_write(&sd_writer, (nomerge
3066 ? NULL((void*)0)
3067 : &sd_reader));
3068 assert(sw_ret != kSDWriteIgnError)((sw_ret != kSDWriteIgnError) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("sw_ret != kSDWriteIgnError"
, "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 3068, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
3069#ifndef UNIX
3070 sd_writer.close(&sd_writer);
3071#endif
3072 if (!nomerge) {
3073 sd_reader.close(&sd_reader);
3074 bool_Bool did_remove = false0;
3075 if (sw_ret == kSDWriteSuccessfull) {
3076#ifdef UNIX
3077 bool_Bool closed = false0;
3078 // For Unix we check the owner of the file. It's not very nice to
3079 // overwrite a users viminfo file after a "su root", with a
3080 // viminfo file that the user can't read.
3081 FileInfo old_info;
3082 if (os_fileinfo((char *)fname, &old_info)) {
3083 if (getuid() == ROOT_UID0) {
3084 if (old_info.stat.st_uid != ROOT_UID0
3085 || old_info.stat.st_gid != getgid()) {
3086 const uv_uid_t old_uid = (uv_uid_t) old_info.stat.st_uid;
3087 const uv_gid_t old_gid = (uv_gid_t) old_info.stat.st_gid;
3088 const int fchown_ret = os_fchown((int) fd, old_uid, old_gid);
3089 sd_writer.close(&sd_writer);
3090 if (fchown_ret != 0) {
3091 EMSG3(_(RNERR "Failed setting uid and gid for file %s: %s"),emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Failed setting uid and gid for file %s: %s"
))), (tempname), (uv_strerror(fchown_ret)))
3092 tempname, os_strerror(fchown_ret))emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Failed setting uid and gid for file %s: %s"
))), (tempname), (uv_strerror(fchown_ret)));

3094 }
3095 closed = true1;
3096 }
3097 } else if (!(old_info.stat.st_uid == getuid()
3098 ? (old_info.stat.st_mode & 0200)
3099 : (old_info.stat.st_gid == getgid()
3100 ? (old_info.stat.st_mode & 0020)
3101 : (old_info.stat.st_mode & 0002)))) {
3102 EMSG2(_("E137: ShaDa file is not writable: %s"), fname)emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E137: ShaDa file is not writable: %s"
))), (fname));
3103 sd_writer.close(&sd_writer);
3104 goto shada_write_file_did_not_remove;
3105 }
3106 }
3107 if (!closed) {
3108 sd_writer.close(&sd_writer);
3109 }
3110#endif
3111 if (vim_rename(tempname, fname)(vim_rename((char_u *)tempname, (char_u *)fname)) == -1) {
3112 EMSG3(_(RNERR "Can't rename ShaDa file from %s to %s!"),emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Can't rename ShaDa file from %s to %s!"
))), (tempname), (fname))
3113 tempname, fname)emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Can't rename ShaDa file from %s to %s!"
))), (tempname), (fname));
3114 } else {
3115 did_remove = true1;
3116 os_remove(tempname);
3117 }
3118 } else {
3119 if (sw_ret == kSDWriteReadNotShada) {
3120 EMSG3(_(RNERR "Did not rename %s because %s "emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Did not rename %s because %s "
"does not looks like a ShaDa file"))), (tempname), (fname))
3121 "does not looks like a ShaDa file"), tempname, fname)emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Did not rename %s because %s "
"does not looks like a ShaDa file"))), (tempname), (fname));
3122 } else {
3123 EMSG3(_(RNERR "Did not rename %s to %s because there were errors "emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Did not rename %s to %s because there were errors "
"during writing it"))), (tempname), (fname))
3124 "during writing it"), tempname, fname)emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Did not rename %s to %s because there were errors "
"during writing it"))), (tempname), (fname));

3126 }
3127 if (!did_remove) {
3128#ifdef UNIX
3129shada_write_file_did_not_remove:
3130#endif
3131 EMSG3(_(RNERR "Do not forget to remove %s or rename it manually to %s."),emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Do not forget to remove %s or rename it manually to %s."

3132 tempname, fname)emsgf((const char *) (gettext((char *)("E136: " "Do not forget to remove %s or rename it manually to %s."

3165
3166static void shada_free_shada_entry(ShadaEntry *const entry)
3167{
3168 if (entry == NULL((void*)0)) {
3169 return;
3170 }
3171 switch (entry->type) {
3172 case kSDItemMissing: {
3173 break;
3174 }
3175 case kSDItemUnknown: {
3176 xfree(entry->data.unknown_item.contents);
3177 break;
3178 }
3179 case kSDItemHeader: {
3180 api_free_dictionary(entry->data.header);
3181 break;
3182 }
3183 case kSDItemChange:
3184 case kSDItemJump:
3185 case kSDItemGlobalMark:
3186 case kSDItemLocalMark: {
3187 dict_unref(entry->data.filemark.additional_data);
3188 xfree(entry->data.filemark.fname);
3189 break;
3190 }
3191 case kSDItemSearchPattern: {
3192 dict_unref(entry->data.search_pattern.additional_data);
3193 xfree(entry->data.search_pattern.pat);
3194 break;
3195 }
3196 case kSDItemRegister: {
3197 dict_unref(entry->data.reg.additional_data);
3198 for (size_t i = 0; i < entry->data.reg.contents_size; i++) {
3199 xfree(entry->data.reg.contents[i]);
3200 }
3201 xfree(entry->data.reg.contents);
3202 break;
3203 }
3204 case kSDItemHistoryEntry: {
3205 list_unref(entry->data.history_item.additional_elements);
3206 xfree(entry->data.history_item.string);
3207 break;
3208 }
3209 case kSDItemVariable: {
3210 list_unref(entry->data.global_var.additional_elements);
3211 xfree(entry->data.global_var.name);
3212 clear_tv(&entry->data.global_var.value);
3213 break;
3214 }
3215 case kSDItemSubString: {
3216 list_unref(entry->data.sub_string.additional_elements);
3217 xfree(entry->data.sub_string.sub);
3218 break;
3219 }
3220 case kSDItemBufferList: {
3221 for (size_t i = 0; i < entry->data.buffer_list.size; i++) {
3222 xfree(entry->data.buffer_list.buffers[i].fname);
3223 dict_unref(entry->data.buffer_list.buffers[i].additional_data);
3224 }
3225 xfree(entry->data.buffer_list.buffers);
3226 break;
3227 }
3228 }
3229}

3232static inline uint64_t be64toh(uint64_t big_endian_64_bits)(__extension__ ({ register unsigned long __v, __x = (uint64_t
big_endian_64_bits); if (__builtin_constant_p (__x)) __v = (
__extension__ ((((__x) & 0xff00000000000000ull) >> 56
) | (((__x) & 0x00ff000000000000ull) >> 40) | (((__x
) & 0x0000ff0000000000ull) >> 24) | (((__x) & 0x000000ff00000000ull
) >> 8) | (((__x) & 0x00000000ff000000ull) <<
8) | (((__x) & 0x0000000000ff0000ull) << 24) | (((
__x) & 0x000000000000ff00ull) << 40) | (((__x) &
0x00000000000000ffull) << 56))); else __asm__ ("bswap %q0"
: "=r" (__v) : "0" (__x)); __v; }))
3233{
3234#ifdef ORDER_BIG_ENDIAN
3235 return big_endian_64_bits;
3236#else
3237 // It may appear that when !defined(ORDER_BIG_ENDIAN) actual order is big
3238 // endian. This variant is suboptimal, but it works regardless of actual
3239 // order.
3240 uint8_t *buf = (uint8_t *) &big_endian_64_bits;
3241 uint64_t ret = 0;
3242 for (size_t i = 8; i; i--) {
3243 ret |= ((uint64_t) buf[i - 1]) << ((8 - i) * 8);
3244 }
3245 return ret;
3246#endif
3247}

3250/// Read given number of bytes into given buffer, display error if needed
3251///
3252/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition.
3253/// @param[out] buffer Where to save the results.
3254/// @param[in] length How many bytes should be read.
3255///
3256/// @return kSDReadStatusSuccess if everything was OK, kSDReadStatusNotShaDa if
3257/// there were not enough bytes to read or kSDReadStatusReadError if
3258/// there was some error while reading.
3259static ShaDaReadResult fread_len(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader,
3260 char *const buffer,
3261 const size_t length)
3262 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
3263{
3264 const ptrdiff_t read_bytes = sd_reader->read(sd_reader, buffer, length);
3265 (void) read_bytes;
3266
3267 if (sd_reader->error != NULL((void*)0)) {
3268 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while reading ShaDa file: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while reading ShaDa file: %s"
)),
3269 sd_reader->error);
3270 return kSDReadStatusReadError;
3271 } else if (sd_reader->eof) {
3272 emsgf(_(RCERR "Error while reading ShaDa file: "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier"))
3273 "last entry specified that it occupies %" PRIu64 " bytes, "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier"))
3274 "but file ended earlier")gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "last entry specified that it occupies %"
"l" "u" " bytes, " "but file ended earlier")),
3275 (uint64_t) length);
3276 return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
3277 }
3278 assert(read_bytes >= 0 && (size_t) read_bytes == length)((read_bytes >= 0 && (size_t) read_bytes == length
) ? (void) (0) : __assert_fail ("read_bytes >= 0 && (size_t) read_bytes == length"
, "/home/travis/build/neovim/bot-ci/build/neovim/src/nvim/shada.c"
, 3278, __PRETTY_FUNCTION__));
3279 return kSDReadStatusSuccess;
3280}

3282/// Read next unsigned integer from file
3283///
3284/// Errors out if the result is not an unsigned integer.
3285///
3286/// Unlike msgpack own function this one works with `FILE *` and reads *exactly*
3287/// as much bytes as needed, making it possible to avoid both maintaining own
3288/// buffer and calling `fseek`.
3289///
3290/// One byte from file stream is always consumed, even if it is not correct.
3291///
3292/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition.
3293/// @param[out] result Location where result is saved.
3294///
3295/// @return kSDReadStatusSuccess if reading was successfull,
3296/// kSDReadStatusNotShaDa if there were not enough bytes to read or
3297/// kSDReadStatusReadError if reading failed for whatever reason.
3298static ShaDaReadResult msgpack_read_uint64(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader,
3299 const int first_char,
3300 uint64_t *const result)
3301 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
3302{
3303 const uintmax_t fpos = sd_reader->fpos - 1;
3304
3305 if (first_char == EOF(-1)) {
3306 if (sd_reader->error) {
3307 emsgf(_(SERR "System error while reading integer from ShaDa file: %s")gettext((char *)("E886: " "System error while reading integer from ShaDa file: %s"
)),
3308 sd_reader->error);
3309 return kSDReadStatusReadError;
3310 } else if (sd_reader->eof) {
3311 emsgf(_(RCERR "Error while reading ShaDa file: "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "expected positive integer at position %"
"l" "u" ", but got nothing"))
3312 "expected positive integer at position %" PRIu64gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "expected positive integer at position %"
"l" "u" ", but got nothing"))
3313 ", but got nothing")gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "expected positive integer at position %"
"l" "u" ", but got nothing")),
3314 (uint64_t) fpos);
3315 return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
3316 }
3317 }
3318
3319 if (~first_char & 0x80) {
3320 // Positive fixnum
3321 *result = (uint64_t) ((uint8_t) first_char);
3322 } else {
3323 size_t length = 0;
3324 switch (first_char) {
3325 case 0xCC: { // uint8
3326 length = 1;
3327 break;
3328 }
3329 case 0xCD: { // uint16
3330 length = 2;
3331 break;
3332 }
3333 case 0xCE: { // uint32
3334 length = 4;
3335 break;
3336 }
3337 case 0xCF: { // uint64
3338 length = 8;
3339 break;
3340 }
3341 default: {
3342 emsgf(_(RCERR "Error while reading ShaDa file: "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "expected positive integer at position %"
"l" "u"))
3343 "expected positive integer at position %" PRIu64)gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "expected positive integer at position %"
"l" "u")),
3344 (uint64_t) fpos);
3345 return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
3346 }
3347 }
3348 uint64_t buf = 0;
3349 char *buf_u8 = (char *) &buf;
3350 ShaDaReadResult fl_ret;
3351 if ((fl_ret = fread_len(sd_reader, &(buf_u8[sizeof(buf)-length]), length))
3352 != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3353 return fl_ret;
3354 }
3355 *result = be64toh(buf)(__extension__ ({ register unsigned long __v, __x = (buf); if
(__builtin_constant_p (__x)) __v = (__extension__ ((((__x) &
0xff00000000000000ull) >> 56) | (((__x) & 0x00ff000000000000ull
) >> 40) | (((__x) & 0x0000ff0000000000ull) >>
24) | (((__x) & 0x000000ff00000000ull) >> 8) | (((
__x) & 0x00000000ff000000ull) << 8) | (((__x) &
0x0000000000ff0000ull) << 24) | (((__x) & 0x000000000000ff00ull
) << 40) | (((__x) & 0x00000000000000ffull) <<
56))); else __asm__ ("bswap %q0" : "=r" (__v) : "0" (__x)); __v
; }));
3356 }
3357 return kSDReadStatusSuccess;
3358}

3360/// Convert or copy and return a string
3361///

3363/// @param[in] str String to convert.
3364/// @param[in] len String length.
3365///

3367static inline char *get_converted_string(const vimconv_T *const sd_conv,

3371{

3374 }
3375 size_t new_len = len;
3376 char *const new_str = string_convert(sd_conv, str, &new_len)((char *)string_convert((vimconv_T *)sd_conv, (char_u *)str, &
new_len));
3377 if (new_str == NULL((void*)0)) {

3515/// Iterate over shada file contents
3516///
3517/// @param[in] sd_reader Structure containing file reader definition.
3518/// @param[out] entry Address where next entry contents will be saved.
3519/// @param[in] flags Flags, determining whether and which items should be
3520/// skipped (see SRNIFlags enum).
3521/// @param[in] max_kbyte If non-zero, skip reading entries which have length
3522/// greater then given.
3523///
3524/// @return Any value from ShaDaReadResult enum.
3525static ShaDaReadResult shada_read_next_item(ShaDaReadDef *const sd_reader,
3526 ShadaEntry *const entry,
3527 const unsigned flags,
3528 const size_t max_kbyte)
3529 FUNC_ATTR_NONNULL_ALL FUNC_ATTR_WARN_UNUSED_RESULT
3530{
3531 ShaDaReadResult ret = kSDReadStatusMalformed;
3532shada_read_next_item_start:
3533 // Set entry type to kSDItemMissing and also make sure that all pointers in
3534 // data union are NULL so they are safe to xfree(). This is needed in case
3535 // somebody calls goto shada_read_next_item_error before anything is set in
3536 // the switch.
3537 memset(entry, 0, sizeof(*entry));
3538 if (sd_reader->eof) {
3539 return kSDReadStatusFinished;
3540 }
3541
3542 // First: manually unpack type, timestamp and length.
3543 // This is needed to avoid both seeking and having to maintain a buffer.
3544 uint64_t type_u64 = (uint64_t) kSDItemMissing;
3545 uint64_t timestamp_u64;
3546 uint64_t length_u64;
3547
3548 const uint64_t initial_fpos = (uint64_t) sd_reader->fpos;
3549 const int first_char = read_char(sd_reader);
3550 if (first_char == EOF(-1) && sd_reader->eof) {
3551 return kSDReadStatusFinished;
3552 }
3553
3554 ShaDaReadResult mru_ret;
3555 if (((mru_ret = msgpack_read_uint64(sd_reader, first_char, &type_u64))
3556 != kSDReadStatusSuccess)
3557 || ((mru_ret = msgpack_read_uint64(sd_reader, read_char(sd_reader),
3558 &timestamp_u64))
3559 != kSDReadStatusSuccess)
3560 || ((mru_ret = msgpack_read_uint64(sd_reader, read_char(sd_reader),
3561 &length_u64))
3562 != kSDReadStatusSuccess)) {
3563 return mru_ret;
3564 }
3565
3566 const size_t length = (size_t) length_u64;
3567 entry->timestamp = (Timestamp) timestamp_u64;
3568
3569 if (type_u64 == 0) {
3570 // kSDItemUnknown cannot possibly pass that far because it is -1 and that
3571 // will fail in msgpack_read_uint64. But kSDItemMissing may and it will
3572 // otherwise be skipped because (1 << 0) will never appear in flags.
3573 emsgf(_(RCERR "Error while reading ShaDa file: "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "there is an item at position %"
"l" "u" " " "that must not be there: Missing items are " "for internal uses only"
))
3574 "there is an item at position %" PRIu64 " "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "there is an item at position %"
"l" "u" " " "that must not be there: Missing items are " "for internal uses only"
))
3575 "that must not be there: Missing items are "gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "there is an item at position %"
"l" "u" " " "that must not be there: Missing items are " "for internal uses only"
))
3576 "for internal uses only")gettext((char *)("E576: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "there is an item at position %"
"l" "u" " " "that must not be there: Missing items are " "for internal uses only"
)),
3577 initial_fpos);
3578 return kSDReadStatusNotShaDa;
3579 }
3580
3581 if ((type_u64 > SHADA_LAST_ENTRY((uint64_t) kSDItemChange)
3582 ? !(flags & kSDReadUnknown)
3583 : !((unsigned) (1 << type_u64) & flags))
3584 || (max_kbyte && length > max_kbyte * 1024)) {
3585 // First entry is unknown or equal to "\n" (10)? Most likely this means that
3586 // current file is not a ShaDa file because first item should normally be
3587 // a header (excluding tests where first item is tested item). Check this by
3588 // parsing entry contents: in non-ShaDa files this will most likely result
3589 // in incomplete MessagePack string.
3590 if (initial_fpos == 0
3591 && (type_u64 == '\n' || type_u64 > SHADA_LAST_ENTRY((uint64_t) kSDItemChange))) {
3592 const ShaDaReadResult spm_ret = shada_parse_msgpack(sd_reader, length,
3593 NULL((void*)0), NULL((void*)0));
3594 if (spm_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3595 return spm_ret;
3596 }
3597 } else {
3598 const ShaDaReadResult srs_ret = sd_reader_skip(sd_reader, length);
3599 if (srs_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3600 return srs_ret;
3601 }
3602 }
3603 goto shada_read_next_item_start;
3604 }
3605
3606 if (type_u64 > SHADA_LAST_ENTRY((uint64_t) kSDItemChange)) {
3607 entry->type = kSDItemUnknown;
3608 entry->data.unknown_item.size = length;
3609 entry->data.unknown_item.type = type_u64;
3610 if (initial_fpos == 0) {
3611 const ShaDaReadResult spm_ret = shada_parse_msgpack(
3612 sd_reader, length, NULL((void*)0), &entry->data.unknown_item.contents);
3613 if (spm_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3614 entry->type = kSDItemMissing;
3615 }
3616 return spm_ret;
3617 } else {
3618 entry->data.unknown_item.contents = xmalloc(length);
3619 const ShaDaReadResult fl_ret = fread_len(
3620 sd_reader, entry->data.unknown_item.contents, length);
3621 if (fl_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3622 shada_free_shada_entry(entry);
3623 entry->type = kSDItemMissing;
3624 }
3625 return fl_ret;
3626 }
3627 }
3628
3629 msgpack_unpacked unpacked;
3630 char *buf = NULL((void*)0);
3631
3632 const ShaDaReadResult spm_ret = shada_parse_msgpack(sd_reader, length,
3633 &unpacked, &buf);
3634 if (spm_ret != kSDReadStatusSuccess) {
3635 ret = spm_ret;
3636 goto shada_read_next_item_error;
3637 }
3638 ret = kSDReadStatusMalformed;
3639 entry->data = sd_default_values[type_u64].data;
3640 switch ((ShadaEntryType) type_u64) {
3641 case kSDItemHeader: {
3642 if (!msgpack_rpc_to_dictionary(&(unpacked.data), &(entry->data.header))) {
3643 emsgf(_(READERR("header", "is not a dictionary"))gettext((char *)("E575: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "header"
" entry at position %" "l" "u" " " "is not a dictionary")), initial_fpos);
3644 goto shada_read_next_item_error;
3645 }
3646 break;
3647 }
3648 case kSDItemSearchPattern: {
3649 if (unpacked.data.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
3650 emsgf(_(READERR("search pattern", "is not a dictionary"))gettext((char *)("E575: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: " "search pattern"
" entry at position %" "l" "u" " " "is not a dictionary")),
3651 initial_fpos);
3652 goto shada_read_next_item_error;
3653 }
3654 garray_T ad_ga;
3655 ga_init(&ad_ga, sizeof(*(unpacked.data.via.map.ptr)), 1);
3656 for (size_t i = 0; i < unpacked.data.via.map.size; i++) {
3657 CHECK_KEY_IS_STR("search pattern")if (unpacked.data.via.map.ptr[i].key.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_STR
) { emsgf(gettext((char *)("E575: " "Error while reading ShaDa file: "
"search pattern" " entry at position %" "l" "u" " " "has key which is not a string"
)), initial_fpos); CLEAR_GA_AND_ERROR_OUT(ad_ga); } else if (
